            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.scrollingStatusText">Scrolling Status Text</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.scrollingStatusText" checked="" id="settings-config-core.scrollingStatusText"></div><p class="hint">Scrolling status text may appear above Tokens or other canvas objects to provide text feedback about changes for that object.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.pixelRatioResolutionScaling">Pixel Ratio Resolution Scaling</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.pixelRatioResolutionScaling" id="settings-config-core.pixelRatioResolutionScaling"></div><p class="hint">Scale the resolution of the game canvas according to the browser's detected pixel ratio. For display devices with high pixel density (like retina displays) this will increase the rendered resolution of the canvas at the expense of application performance. Resolution scaling is also impacted by the zoom level of the browser or operating system display settings. In such cases this setting will increase or decrease the effective resolution of the canvas depending on the amount of zoom that is applied. Disabling this setting may improve performance at the expense of visual quality for high pixel density displays.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.leftClickRelease">Left-Click to Release Objects</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.leftClickRelease" checked="" id="settings-config-core.leftClickRelease"></div><p class="hint">When enabled, a left click on empty canvas space will release any currently controlled objects. If disabled, objects are released by selecting an empty space, shift-clicking the object, or pressing the escape key.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.performanceMode">Performance Mode</label><div class="form-fields"><select name="core.performanceMode" data-dtype="Number" id="settings-config-core.performanceMode"><option value="0">Low</option><option value="1" selected="">Medium</option><option value="2">High</option><option value="3">Maximum</option></select></div><p class="hint">Choose a performance mode which affects canvas rendering quality and application performance. Lower performance modes will work better for less powerful hardware.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.maxFPS">Maximum Framerate</label><div class="form-fields"><range-picker name="core.maxFPS" value="40" min="10" max="60" step="10" id="settings-config-core.maxFPS"><input type="range" min="10" max="60" step="10"><input type="number" min="10" max="60" step="10"></range-picker></div><p class="hint">Limit the maximum framerate at which Foundry Virtual Tabletop will render canvas updates. Lowering this value may improve application performance for less powerful hardware.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.photosensitiveMode">Photosensitivity Mode</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.photosensitiveMode" id="settings-config-core.photosensitiveMode"></div><p class="hint">Enabling this mode reduces the prevalence and intensity of flashing, fast-moving, and repetitive animations and effects.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.tokenAutoRotate">Automatic Token Rotation</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.tokenAutoRotate" checked="" id="settings-config-core.tokenAutoRotate"></div><p class="hint">When enabled, Tokens are automatically rotated in the direction of movement by default. Regardless of this setting, the Lock Rotation setting on individual tokens will still prevent their artwork from being visually rotated.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.tokenDragPreview">Token Drag Vision</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.tokenDragPreview" checked="" id="settings-config-core.tokenDragPreview"></div><p class="hint">When enabled, vision and lighting for a Token is previewed in real time during a left-click drag workflow. This is disabled by default because it may promote undesirable meta-gaming behaviors.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.visionAnimation">Token Vision Animation</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.visionAnimation" checked="" id="settings-config-core.visionAnimation"></div><p class="hint">Animate Token vision and light changes during Token movement animations. Disabling this will improve performance for lower-end machines.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.lightAnimation">Light Source Animation</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.lightAnimation" checked="" id="settings-config-core.lightAnimation"></div><p class="hint">Allow light source animations. Disabling this will improve performance for lower-end machines.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.mipmap">Zoomed Texture Antialiasing</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="core.mipmap" checked="" id="settings-config-core.mipmap"></div><p class="hint">Compute mipmaps to antialias sprite textures at lower levels of zoom.             <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.editorAutosaveSecs">Editor Autosave Frequency</label><div class="form-fields"><range-picker name="core.editorAutosaveSecs" value="30" min="30" max="300" step="10" id="settings-config-core.editorAutosaveSecs"><input type="range" min="30" max="300" step="10"><input type="number" min="30" max="300" step="10"></range-picker></div><p class="hint">The number of seconds between each autosave for any open ProseMirror editor.</p></div>

            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-core.gridDiagonals">Grid Diagonals</label><div class="form-fields"><select name="core.gridDiagonals" data-dtype="Number" id="settings-config-core.gridDiagonals"><option value="0" selected="">Equidistant (1)</option><option value="1">Exact (√2)</option><option value="2">Approximate (1.5)</option><option value="3">Rectilinear (2)</option><option value="4">Alternating (1/2/1)</option><option value="5">Alternating (2/1/2)</option><option value="6">Illegal (∞)</option></select></div><p class="hint">Configure how diagonal distance is measured on square and hexagonal grids.         <section class="tab scrollable active" data-group="categories" data-tab="coffee-pub-blacksmith" data-category="coffee-pub-blacksmith">
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH1GettingStarted">Getting Started</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="text" name="coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH1GettingStarted" value="" id="settings-config-coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH1GettingStarted"></div><p class="hint">Essential settings to get started with Coffee Pub Blacksmith</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH4Introduction">Introduction</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="text" name="coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH4Introduction" value="" id="settings-config-coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH4Introduction"></div><p class="hint">The Blacksmith Module serves as the foundational framework for the entire Coffee Pub module series, providing essential services and shared functionality that all other modules depend upon. While powerful as a standalone module with features like enhanced combat statistics, customizable UI elements, and comprehensive token management, its true potential is realized when integrated with the complete Coffee Pub suite, where it orchestrates seamless communication and synchronization between all modules.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH2CoffeePubSuite">Coffee Pub Suite</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="text" name="coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH2CoffeePubSuite" value="" id="settings-config-coffee-pub-blacksmith.headingH2CoffeePubSuite"></div><p class="hint">Information about installed Coffee Pub modules</p></div>

If you don't see a module you are expecting, check to see if you've activated it.</p></div>

            <div class="form-group">
                <label>3D Dice Settings</label>
                <div class="form-fields">
                    <button type="button" data-action="openSubmenu" data-key="dice-so-nice.dice-so-nice">            <i class="fas fa-dice-d20" inert=""></i>
            <span>3D Dice Settings</span>
                    </button>
                </div>    <p class="hint">This is where each player can configure their own individual 3D dice settings (enable/disable, colors, size, performances…)</p>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <label>Rollable Area Settings</label>
                <div class="form-fields">
                    <button type="button" data-action="openSubmenu" data-key="dice-so-nice.rollable-area">            <i class="fas fa-crop-alt" inert=""></i>
            <span>Rollable Area Settings</span>
                    </button>
                </div>    <p class="hint">Define the portion of the screen that shows the 3D dice animation. This setting won't affect other players.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.maxDiceNumber">Max Number of Dice</label><div class="form-fields"><range-picker name="dice-so-nice.maxDiceNumber" value="20" min="20" max="100" step="5" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.maxDiceNumber"><input type="range" min="20" max="100" step="5"><input type="number" min="20" max="100" step="5"></range-picker></div><p class="hint">Maximum number of displayed dice in an animation. Higher numbers will reduce performances</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.globalAnimationSpeed">Global animation speed</label><div class="form-fields"><select name="dice-so-nice.globalAnimationSpeed" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.globalAnimationSpeed"><option value="0" selected="">Players' choice</option><option value="1">Normal</option><option value="2">2x</option><option value="3">3x</option></select></div><p class="hint">Set the animation speed for all players instead of using their own settings</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.resetWelcomeMessage">Reset welcome message</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.resetWelcomeMessage" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.resetWelcomeMessage"></div><p class="hint">This will reset the welcome message for all players. They'll see the welcome message again the next time they join this world.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.enabledSimultaneousRolls">Simultaneous rolls are merged</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.enabledSimultaneousRolls" checked="" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.enabledSimultaneousRolls"></div><p class="hint">Combine simultaneous rolls from different actions in a single animation instead of waiting for each roll to end.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.enabledSimultaneousRollForMessage">Same-message rolls are merged</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.enabledSimultaneousRollForMessage" checked="" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.enabledSimultaneousRollForMessage"></div><p class="hint">When a single message contains multiple rolls, play all simultaneously</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.diceCanBeFlipped">Dice can be flipped</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.diceCanBeFlipped" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.diceCanBeFlipped"></div><p class="hint">When a die has finished rolling, can it be flipped by newly added rolling dice (This does not change the result).</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.disabledDuringCombat">Disabled during combat</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.disabledDuringCombat" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.disabledDuringCombat"></div><p class="hint">Disable 3D dice roll animations while a combat is active.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.disabledForInitiative">Disabled for Initiative rolls</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.disabledForInitiative" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.disabledForInitiative"></div><p class="hint">Disable 3D dice roll when rolling initiative from the combat tracker.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.forceCharacterOwnerAppearanceForInitiative">Use owner dice for initiative</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.forceCharacterOwnerAppearanceForInitiative" checked="" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.forceCharacterOwnerAppearanceForInitiative"></div><p class="hint">When enabled, use the character owner's dice appearance when rolling initiative from the combat tracker regardless of the roll author (ie:GM).</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.immediatelyDisplayChatMessages">Display chat message immediately</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.immediatelyDisplayChatMessages" checked="" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.immediatelyDisplayChatMessages"></div><p class="hint">When enabled, do not wait for the 3D roll to finish before showing the roll chat card</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.animateRollTable">Enable 3D dice on Roll Tables</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.animateRollTable" checked="" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.animateRollTable"></div><p class="hint">Show a 3D dice when rolling on a Roll Table. Need 'Animate roll tables' to 'off' in the core settings and 'Display Formula to Chat' to 'off' in the Roll Table.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.animateInlineRoll">Enable 3D dice on Inline Rolls</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.animateInlineRoll" checked="" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.animateInlineRoll"></div><p class="hint">When possible, show 3D dice when an inline roll is detected in the chat.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.hideNpcRolls">Disable 3D dice on NPC rolls</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.hideNpcRolls" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.hideNpcRolls"></div><p class="hint">Don't show 3D dice for any roll coming from an NPC.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.allowInteractivity">Allow interaction with rolled dice</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.allowInteractivity" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.allowInteractivity"></div><p class="hint">Let players grab and throw 3D dice after they've been rolled on the table (this has no effect on the results)</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.hide3dDiceOnSecretRolls">Hide 3D dice on GM/Blind rolls</label><div class="form-fields"><input type="checkbox" name="dice-so-nice.hide3dDiceOnSecretRolls" checked="" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.hide3dDiceOnSecretRolls"></div><p class="hint">Do not display 3D dice to other players on GM/Blind rolls.</p></div>
            <div class="form-group"><label for="settings-config-dice-so-nice.showGhostDice">Show Ghost dice for hidden rolls</label><div class="form-fields"><select name="dice-so-nice.showGhostDice" id="settings-config-dice-so-nice.showGhostDice"><option value="0">Disable Ghost dice</option><option value="1" selected="">To all players</option><option value="2">To the roll author only</option></select></div><p class="hint">When possible, show a dice without numbers to players when rolling a GM or Blind roll.</p></div>
        </section>
